   window.addEventListener ("message", function (event) {
      if (! event ||! event.data)
        return;
      try {
        var data = window.JSON.parse (event.data);
        var iframes = document.querySelectorAll ('iframe [src * = "' + data.url + '"]');

        if (iframes.length> 0) {
          var height = "" + data.height;
          if (! height.includes ("px")) {
            height + = "px";
          }

          for (var i = 0; i <iframes.length; i ++) {
            iframes [i] .style ['height'] = height;
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {
        // wrong message format (no JSON)
      }
    }, false);
  </script>

     <section class = "iph-wrapper iph-wrapper - backgroundLight iph-wrapper - has-border-top iph-padding-top-xxl iph-padding-bottom-xxl iph-footer__footnotes-and-legaltext" data-footnotes- url = "/ content / iph / market_de / DEU60992 / de / jcr: content / footer.footnoteContent.json" id = "footnotesid">
      <div class = "iph-grid-container">
       <div class = "iph-row">
        <div class = "iph-column">
         <section class = "iph-footnotes" data-component-id = "/ content / iph / market_de / DEU60992 / de / jcr: content / footer" data-component-name = "disclaimer-and-footnotes" data-component- version = "1604071773545-1602760359296">
         </section>
        </div>
        <div class = "iph-column">
         <div class = "iph-legaltext" data-component-id = "/ content / iph / market_de / DEU60992 / de / jcr: content / footer / guide" data-component-name = "legal-text" data-component- version = "1604071773545-1602760359388">
          <p>
           * The stated consumption and emission values ‚Äã‚Äãwere determined according to the legally prescribed measuring procedure. Since September 1, 2017, certain new vehicles have been type-approved according to the Worldwide Harmonized Light Vehicles Test Procedure (WLTP), a more realistic test procedure for measuring fuel consumption and CO2 emissions. From September 1, 2018, the WLTP will gradually replace the new European driving cycle (NEDC). Due to the more realistic test conditions, the fuel consumption and CO2 emission values ‚Äã‚Äãmeasured according to the WLTP are in many cases higher than those measured according to the NEDC. This may result in corresponding changes in vehicle taxation from September 1, 2018. For more information on the differences between WLTP and NEDC, see
           <a href="https://www.audi.de/de/brand/de/neuwagen/layer/wltp-lp.html?partner_id=60992" target="_blank">
            www.audi.de/wltp.
           </a>
          </p>
          <p>
           Currently, the NEDC values ‚Äã‚Äãare still mandatory to communicate. As far as new cars are concerned that are type-approved according to WLTP, the NEDC values ‚Äã‚Äãare derived from the WLTP values. The additional specification of the WLTP values ‚Äã‚Äãcan be made voluntarily until their use is mandatory. Insofar as the NEDC values ‚Äã‚Äãare given as ranges, they do not refer to a single, individual vehicle and are not part of the offer. They are used solely for purposes of comparison between the various vehicle types. Additional equipment and accessories (attachments, tire format, etc.) can include relevant vehicle parameters, such as B. change weight, rolling resistance and aerodynamics and, in addition to weather and traffic conditions as well as individual driving behavior, influence fuel consumption, electricity consumption, CO2 emissions and the mileage of a vehicle.
          </p>
          <p>
           Further information on the official fuel consumption and the official specific CO2 emissions of new passenger cars can be found in the "Guide to fuel consumption, CO2 emissions and power consumption of new passenger cars", which is available at all sales outlets and at DAT Deutsche Automobil Treuhand GmbH, Hellmuth- Hirth-Str. 1, D-73760 Ostfildern or at
           <a href="https://www.dat.de/leitfaden/LeitfadenCO2.pdf" target="_blank">
            www.dat.de
           </a>
           is available free of charge.
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </section>
